
# Validation plots for SModelS-v3.1.2fast

This page lists validation plots for all analyses and topologies available in
the SMS results database that can be validated against official results.
Superseded results are listed; fastlim results are not. The list has been created from the
database version 3.1.2fast, including the Fastlim tarball that is shipped separately.
There is also a [list of all analyses](ListOfAnalyses312fast), 
a list of [all SMS topologies](SmsDictionary312fast), and an explicit [comparison of best-SR vs combined-SR](ExclComparison312fast) exclusion lines.

The validation procedure for upper limit maps used here is explained in [arXiv:1312.4175](http://arxiv.org/abs/1312.4175),  [EPJC May 2014, 74:2868](http://link.springer.com/article/10.1140/epjc/s10052-014-2868-5), section 4. For validating efficiency maps, a very similar procedure is followed. For every input point, the best signal region is chosen. If a covariance matrix has been published, we present the combined limit of all signal regions. The experimental upper limits are compared with the theoretical predictions for that signal region.

Note that the SModelS validation plots show on- and off-shell regions
separately (e.g., T2tt and T2ttoff) while the exclusion lines given by ATLAS or
CMS are for on- and off-shell at once.


To [official validation plots](Validation312fast)

## Individual tables

### Run 2 - 13 TeV
 * [ATLAS efficiency maps](#ATLASefficiencymaps13): 37 analyses (1 new/updated), 37 results (1 new/updated)
 * [ATLAS upper limits](#ATLASupperlimits13): 42 analyses (no new/updated), 42 results (no new/updated)
 * [CMS efficiency maps](#CMSefficiencymaps13): 11 analyses (no new/updated), 11 results (no new/updated)
 * [CMS upper limits](#CMSupperlimits13): 52 analyses (no new/updated), 52 results (no new/updated)

### Run 1 - 8 TeV
 * [ATLAS efficiency maps](#ATLASefficiencymaps8): 11 analyses (no new/updated), 11 results (no new/updated)
 * [ATLAS upper limits](#ATLASupperlimits8): 34 analyses (no new/updated), 34 results (no new/updated)
 * [CMS efficiency maps](#CMSefficiencymaps8): 10 analyses (no new/updated), 10 results (no new/updated)
 * [CMS upper limits](#CMSupperlimits8): 22 analyses (no new/updated), 22 results (no new/updated)
